Analyze the animation architecture and identify foundational improvement opportunities. Focus on:

1. **Code duplication patterns** - repetitive logic across theaters/components
2. **Composable extraction opportunities** - shared animation logic that could be abstracted
3. **Component composition issues** - places where theaters could be broken into smaller, reusable pieces
